  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_2cf4ef85-44dc-4814-b4a4-a7e31dca8d19'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initializeSiwa();

    <div class="section firstReview">
      

<div id="review_1242075499" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1242075499" />
    <a title="Jasmine" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12113097-jasmine"><img alt="Jasmine" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1548531522p2/12113097.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1242075499?book_show_action=true">Mar 31, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jasmine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jasmine" href="/user/show/12113097-jasmine">Jasmine</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1242075499" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1177886120539309118">I know most of you will be disappointed in me since I've basically built up this sarcastic, harsh, hateful, and slightly aloof persona. And here I am putting this book on my I-Want-it-Like-I-Want-Food shelf (which is a very serious shelf). But I have a confession to make — a confession that will destroy this façade I've spent so long building up with just one sentence; <br/><br/>I love watching DanIsNotOnFire and AmazingPhil on Youtube. <br/><blockquote>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427837499ra/14326667.gif' width='350' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</blockquote><br/>Yep. I've lost all of my critical credibility (however small). Bu</span>
  <span id="freeText1177886120539309118" style="display:none">I know most of you will be disappointed in me since I've basically built up this sarcastic, harsh, hateful, and slightly aloof persona. And here I am putting this book on my I-Want-it-Like-I-Want-Food shelf (which is a very serious shelf). But I have a confession to make — a confession that will destroy this façade I've spent so long building up with just one sentence; <br><br>I love watching DanIsNotOnFire and AmazingPhil on Youtube. <br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427837499ra/14326667.gif" width="350" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br>Yep. I've lost all of my critical credibility (however small). But you know what? Frankly, my dear reader, I don't give a damn. Whenever I watch either Dan or Phil they always manage to make me happy, and that's all that should matter. So that is why on the 8th of October, I will walk into a bookstore and nab this book off of the shelf because I know that whatever in it will surly make me smile. Plus, it has artwork by the artist who worked on one of my favourite British comedy series, <i>The Mighty Boosh</i>. Damn straight I'm buying this. <br><br>So to all those people who now think I have an immature sense of humour;<br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427837868ra/14326710.gif" width="350" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="1177886120539309118" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1305601063" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1305601063" />
    <a title="Maria (Big City Bookworm)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2567068-maria-big-city-bookworm"><img alt="Maria (Big City Bookworm)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1558875339p2/2567068.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1305601063?book_show_action=true">Jun 11, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maria (Big City Bookworm)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maria (Big City Bookworm)" href="/user/show/2567068-maria-big-city-bookworm">Maria (Big City Bookworm)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9781101939840" href="/book/show/25489156-the-amazing-book-is-not-on-fire">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2567068-maria-big-city-bookworm?shelf=2015-new-releases">2015-new-releases</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2567068-maria-big-city-bookworm?shelf=read-2015">read-2015</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1305601063" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10425368473815874645"><b>4.5 stars</b><br/><br/>If you came here looking for an in depth review, you came to the wrong place. The Amazing Book Is Not On Fire is completely random and fun and crazy and so I figured this review should be the same.<br/><br/>For those of you are are unfamiliar with Dan Howell (Danisnotonfire) and Phil Lester (AmazingPhil) you probably don't spend a lot of time watching vloggers in the wonderful world of YouTube. I remember way back when I had first heard of Youtube, I was in Grade 9, which was 10 years ago (I know</span>
  <span id="freeText10425368473815874645" style="display:none"><b>4.5 stars</b><br /><br />If you came here looking for an in depth review, you came to the wrong place. The Amazing Book Is Not On Fire is completely random and fun and crazy and so I figured this review should be the same.<br /><br />For those of you are are unfamiliar with Dan Howell (Danisnotonfire) and Phil Lester (AmazingPhil) you probably don't spend a lot of time watching vloggers in the wonderful world of YouTube. I remember way back when I had first heard of Youtube, I was in Grade 9, which was 10 years ago (I know, I'm old as hell), and one of my friends had shown me a video on this weird website called YouTube. It wouldn't be until a few years later when I really started to follow different Youtubers such as Shane Dawson, Smosh and the Shaytards. Fast forward a few more years and it seemed as though the equivalent of the British Invasion in the 1960's was now taking place on YouTube. The Brits started popping up everywhere with YouTubers such as Zoella and JacksGap. A popular thing for Youtubers to do is to work together on collaboration videos, or "collabs"...one thing led to another, and I discovered Dan and Phil! Before I discovered their individual channels, I came across videos they made together in a series called "Phil is Not on Fire". As I would later learn by reading The Amazing Book Is Not On Fire, Dan and Phil's personal channels (Danisnotonfire and AmazingPhil) had been a part of the YouTube community for almost its entire existence and unfortunately I discovered them pretty late in the game. Better late than never though, am I right?<br /><br />Although I am subscribed to quite a few YouTubers, there are only a few that I watch on a regular basis. Considering the crazy amount of books by YouTubers that have been released recently, there are only a few that I would really care to read. Dan and Phil had quickly become two of my favourite YouTubers and when they announced they would be releasing a book together, I knew that it was one that I needed to read.<br /><br />I think part of what makes Dan and Phil so great is the fact that they're relatable. They are huge nerds and they aren't afraid to hide that about themselves. They're quirky and hilarious to watch on screen and their book was no different. The Amazing Book Is Not On Fire feels like one of Dan and Phil's videos, but in book form. That's the only way I can describe it. It's random and cute and hilarious, which is exactly how I feel about the content they upload to YouTube. There were quite a few personal stories which gave us some insight into their early lives and how they got started in the YouTube community. I loved getting to know them through this book.<br /><br />The book itself is physically very appealing. Like I stated earlier, there have been an endless amount of books released by YouTubers recently and I hate to say it, but they all look like the same old autobiography with a few coloured photograph pages in the middle. Although I'm sure their personal stories would be great to hear, the books themselves aren't very unique in appearance. The Amazing Book Is Not On Fire completely defied the stereotype that is an autobiography. The entire book is fully coloured and filled with endless amounts of photographs, doodles and other fancy little tidbits. We get actual scanned images from both Dan and Phil's old diaries as well as fun little quizzes and micro stories mixed in with personal experiences. It's a pretty refreshing format compared to just having a bunch of words on a page and that definitely helps make it stand out.<br /><br />Dan and Phil have done an amazing job in creating this book. They even thought of their viewers while creating the book and made a fantastic little video on their YouTube channel showing the entire process. Even if you don't enjoy the idea of reading a book created by a YouTuber, I suggest diving in to the world of YouTube itself! I know that YouTube, and subscribing to certain YouTubers, is an acquired taste that isn't meant for everyone, but I guarantee if you look hard enough, there is bound to be at least one YouTuber that you find relatable and entertaining. </span>
  <a data-text-id="10425368473815874645" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1304588328" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1304588328" />
    <a title="Mal" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5228441-mal"><img alt="Mal" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577606473p2/5228441.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1304588328?book_show_action=true">Jun 10, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mal" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mal" href="/user/show/5228441-mal">Mal</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5228441-mal?shelf=own">own</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1304588328" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8020478525290262878">Before: <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[Dan and Phil are my life.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434990595ra/15288311.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I don't particularly want to read any books written by youtubers, and never really care so much when they announce the books existence -- but I screamed so loud when I saw their announcement video. <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><br/>**probably some spoilers? <s>can you spoil memoirs</s>**<br/><br/>Prior to the Amazing Book is Not on Fire announcement I didn't ever really want to read books written by YouTubers. Or ... any memoirs, or life-stories, for that matter. They seemed to close</span>
  <span id="freeText8020478525290262878" style="display:none">Before: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Dan and Phil are my life.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434990595ra/15288311.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I don't particularly want to read any books written by youtubers, and never really care so much when they announce the books existence -- but I screamed so loud when I saw their announcement video. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>**probably some spoilers? <s>can you spoil memoirs</s>**<br><br>Prior to the Amazing Book is Not on Fire announcement I didn't ever really want to read books written by YouTubers. Or ... any memoirs, or life-stories, for that matter. They seemed to closely related to the non-fiction genre (and let's be real, that is definitely not the most engaging source of entertainment), but by the time Dan and Phil posted the announcement video ... I was a diehard Phan. They're pretty much the only YouTubers I watch anymore -- save for Connor, and Tyler and Pewds on special occasions. This book was suddenly something that I <i>had</i> to read. I had to have it. I would have gotten it the second it came out if I could have, but Christmas was around the corner and in our house buying things just before Christmas is basically like a focial (family social. I just made that up 10/10) suicide. I should have ordered it. <br><br><b>Regardless.</b> <br><br>I satisfied my unholy need for the book by reading Connors book and then realizing that Tyler was on the verge of releasing his own. Thanks, Dan &amp; Phil. This is your fault. Now I have more books to procrastinate reading. Of course, when I finally picked this one up -- literally yesterday -- I finished it right away. It's kind of perfect. I mean, it's so <i>them.</i> There is nothing in this book that I can't picture them saying or doing. Tbh I read like 95% of this in two vaguely different, but both equally bad, British accents? I spent most of today at home alone so I guess talking to myself isn't that shameful, no one heard. Even if they had something in me doubts they would think this is a very un-Mal like thing to do <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">["What's that sound?" "She's probably just talking to herself." "Why is she British?" "*shrug* I learned to just roll with it" <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. This acceptance is probably because like everyone in my family does this. Like, I'll be sitting in my room and my brother is making explosion sounds in the shower just across the hallway (I'm being completely serious rn).<br> <br>Back on topic~! I cried a little when they were talking about meeting One Direction -- wow, Dan, I didn't know you were so passionate about the boys -- and their trip to Japan; I had to harden my emotions and stop crying or I'd never get through it. To clarify I was crying because I was laughing so hard. I guess you probably already knew that. Anyway... some of the best parts of this book, I think, were:<br><blockquote>
<b>1.</b> The Phanga. They made a literal graphic strip about their becoming magical boys, and Phil had a lowkey crush on the president of the cereal club (whom, I may add, was carrying around a handy carton of milk) and was just like notice me cereal-senpai. And it was pretty wonderful. Also, that fringe-check tho. <br><b>2.</b> Phanfiction. Naturally Dan writes a three page long dark, depressing, really intense fic about vampires and Phil writes a one page long <i>to-be-continued</i> story in which he gives birth to Harry Styles. This says so much about them, really and truly. <br><b>3.</b> Reasons why Dan is a Fail / Things that Phil thought were true that weren't really true. Some of my favorite videos turned into two colored pages of heaven.<br><b>4.</b> THEY WENT TO A FUCKING MAID CAFE AND DAN SELFIED WITH RIN WHAT IS MY LIFE I WANNA DO THAT TOO.</blockquote><br><br>Also this book is extra special to me because this is the 700th book on my read list. I've read 700 books :o<br><br><br><b>3/19:</b> MAL GETS TO SEE DAN AND PHIL ON TOUR THIS SUMMER WHOOOOO. </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="8020478525290262878" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1415673491" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1415673491" />
    <a title="Elly (imaginemorebooks)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27877374-elly-imaginemorebooks"><img alt="Elly (imaginemorebooks)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1563059662p2/27877374.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1415673491?book_show_action=true">Oct 13, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Elly (imaginemorebooks)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Elly (imaginemorebooks)" href="/user/show/27877374-elly-imaginemorebooks">Elly (imaginemorebooks)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1415673491" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3723757344605428116">I wasn't sure what I was expecting when I first watched the trailer for this book back in March. I just instantly knew I needed to have it the second it was released. Dan and Phil are two of my favorite youtubers that I have been following for years so obviously I ended up reading this book in one sitting. <br/>Overall, I have a lot of mixed feelings about this book. I guess the most prominent is that this book was made for the fans (and Dan and Phil themselves). Simply put, it is like a scrapbook th</span>
  <span id="freeText3723757344605428116" style="display:none">I wasn't sure what I was expecting when I first watched the trailer for this book back in March. I just instantly knew I needed to have it the second it was released. Dan and Phil are two of my favorite youtubers that I have been following for years so obviously I ended up reading this book in one sitting. <br />Overall, I have a lot of mixed feelings about this book. I guess the most prominent is that this book was made for the fans (and Dan and Phil themselves). Simply put, it is like a scrapbook that visually displays who Dan and Phil are and what they have created on the Internet. I don't anticipate random people buying this book in a shop, reading it and enjoying it. It almost feels like a behind the scenes of their videos. You get the condensed version of the brand they have created with just a little extra thrown in. <br />For me, it felt like I had just rematched some of their best videos. The whole book is basically rehashing the last six years they have been in each other's lives. Being someone who watches them religiously, I was a bit disappointed in that. I was hoping for a book full of new content, not old content that I already had memorized. That being said, there were a few new things that I really enjoyed. Some of my favorite parts where the quick mentions of things you didn't know before or the pages where they are "going deep". I also REALLY enjoyed Dan's fanfic. Damn, that boy can write. <br />I guess what I'm trying to say is that I wish this book was more of a serious "this is me, I'm more than Phan and cat whiskers". However, I do still appreciate all that this book is. This book is Dan and Phil, every cringey bit of them. Take the best bits of all their videos and sprinkle it with some extra existential crisis and general Phil weirdness and you have TABINOF. It really is just a tangible version of their online content, which to be fair is exactly what they marketed it as. <br />If you are a fan of the kind of content Dan and Phil make, by all means pick up this book! It's as quirky and interesting as they are. But, if you don't know who they are or don't obsess over their videos, I don't see you enjoying this book. It's a book about the online world and community Dan and Phil have created and if you aren't already in on all the jokes the whole book probably all just seems a bit strange. I mean, what isn't strange about two men who draw cat whiskers on their faces, roll around and talk to a camera for a living?</span>
  <a data-text-id="3723757344605428116" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1506006456" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9657133437124690410">Quick review for a quick read. Yes, I subscribe to both Danisnotonfire and AmazingPhil (as well as their gaming channel - because Dan falling out of his chair playing FNAF still makes me laugh. I have no shame.). That's how I ended up figuring out that they released a book - but I didn't realize they had an audiobook version until browsing Audible. I had a credit, I used it on this book - I regret nothing.<br/><br/>This was such a fun read. I was entertained not just learning a bit from their random games</span>
  <span id="freeText9657133437124690410" style="display:none">Quick review for a quick read. Yes, I subscribe to both Danisnotonfire and AmazingPhil (as well as their gaming channel - because Dan falling out of his chair playing FNAF still makes me laugh. I have no shame.). That's how I ended up figuring out that they released a book - but I didn't realize they had an audiobook version until browsing Audible. I had a credit, I used it on this book - I regret nothing.<br /><br />This was such a fun read. I was entertained not just learning a bit from their random games (i.e. favorite emojis, 7-second challenge, A-Z lists) and experiences (the craziness of meeting One Direction included), but also just learning about the two of these guys in general. The book is structured from their high school and college experiences, to getting their own radio show, to traveling to Japan, among other major themes, but they're not afraid to go in random directions, which are so much fun to listen to. My first listen in 2016, and one of my favorite reads thus far this year.<br /><br />Overall score: 4.5/5 stars</span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/48295288-lia?shelf=non-fiction">non-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/48295288-lia?shelf=english-and-american-lit-and-more">english-and-american-lit-and-more</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/48295288-lia?shelf=humor">humor</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1579721068" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4594251830392986610">I'm having a really productive day that so far has mainly consisted of me <a href='https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=98BM_66MMCA' rel='nofollow noopener'>thrashing around in bed and feeling sorry for myself</a> and <a href='https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=_h17_0pyIu4' rel='nofollow noopener'>overdosing on aspirin while coughing my lungs out.</a> Good times. <br/><br/>*awkwardly clears throat*<br/><br/>Well, hello everybody! It is Giulia here, and welcome to what you all secretly wanted but didn't know you needed: <b>THE INTERACTIVE REVIEW.</b> (If you haven't already noticed my sneaky move, those up there were links you were supposed to click on. Duh.)<br/><br/>Now, the most sensible thing to d</span>
  <span id="freeText4594251830392986610" style="display:none">I'm having a really productive day that so far has mainly consisted of me <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=98BM_66MMCA" rel="nofollow noopener">thrashing around in bed and feeling sorry for myself</a> and <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=_h17_0pyIu4" rel="nofollow noopener">overdosing on aspirin while coughing my lungs out.</a> Good times. <br><br>*awkwardly clears throat*<br><br>Well, hello everybody! It is Giulia here, and welcome to what you all secretly wanted but didn't know you needed: <b>THE INTERACTIVE REVIEW.</b> (If you haven't already noticed my sneaky move, those up there were links you were supposed to click on. Duh.)<br><br>Now, the most sensible thing to do right now would be to say that this is obviously a book aimed solely to Dan and Phil fans... <b>But.</b> What kind of dedicated, mildly crazy and obsessed fan would <i>I</i> be if I didn't at least try to lure you into joining the dark side, also known as the phandom?<br>You get the idea. So, without further ado... let's get started.<br><br>I hereby introduce you to Dan Howell, British Youtuber and socially awkward nerd with some unexpectedly deep thoughts in that creative mind of his.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1461085889ra/18822436.gif" width="350" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And here we have Phil Lester, also a British Youtuber, with a (former) Northern accent and a positive attitude that is 100% guaranteed to brighten even your bleakest day.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1461085889ra/18822437.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>Now, for a lot of us Youtube is that quiet, peaceful place where we can escape the - boring - real world and either have some fun, be inspired, discover new things and generally be entertained. *insert generic vlog music here* Personally, <a href="https://www.youtube.com/user/danisnotonfire" rel="nofollow noopener">Dan</a> and <a href="https://www.youtube.com/user/AmazingPhil" rel="nofollow noopener">Phil</a> do not only always manage to make me smile, but have genuinely helped me go through some difficult times in my life, turning my sad frown into hysterical laughter (yes, Phil.) and making me realize that sometimes it's okay to have no idea where you're going in life, and it's not the end of the world (yes, Dan.) *generic music turns slightly more dramatic* But I will explain all of this later. <br><br><br><br>• If you, like me, are a proud nerd, crazy fangirl, tumblr addict or just a generally awkward person that is not sure how to function in society, please go to <b>POINT 1.</b><br><br>• If you, also like me, live your life in a constant state of existential crisis, wondering what the point in life is and questioning your life choices every 5 minutes, please go to <b>POINT 2.</b> <br><br>• If you're having a shitty day and your face cannot honestly remember what it means to smile, please go to <b>POINT 3.</b> (Oh, and eat some chocolate. That always helps.)<br><br>• If you're the kind of really curious person that has always loved to travel and see new places in the world, please go to <b>POINT 4.</b><br><br>• And if you want a little preview of the actual book to get a feel of what you're getting into, then please go to <b>POINT 5.</b><br><br><br><br><br><br><b>1)</b> <br>Okay, I'm assuming that by now all the weird people that think that social interaction is actually fun (???) and that <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=9fl7nHK7GtY&amp;list=PLXz7yWsG69-bSlDd_tr66JSgl2Xub2M5F" rel="nofollow noopener">don't know what tumblr is</a> and find themselves asking <i>what does OTP mean?</i> with wide eyes have left, so just between us nerds... trust me, you need Dan and Phil in your life. Not only because we all speak the same language - what? No, of course I don't mean English. I mean <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=r5m3xYLGnVM" rel="nofollow noopener">the language of memes.</a> I'm surprised you even had to ask - but also because it's pretty nice to know that even if <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=tFPF7qk5l6w" rel="nofollow noopener">you sometimes do incredibly awkward and embarrassing things</a> and <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=49Y-BM7fnM4&amp;list=PLD397AA0478943319&amp;index=6" rel="nofollow noopener">feel like you're literally failing at normal human interaction</a>... well, that's not necessarily a bad thing. Okay, sadly you <i>still</i> need to <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=iVR4pIQy-dU" rel="nofollow noopener">get out of bed and go adulting</a>, but there's nothing wrong with feeling lazy and not being one of those people who practice 5 sports, have a dream job and own a summer house in California. (Though I wouldn't mind having that last one. Yeah.) (Also, here's a little treat for all of us <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=lJSu9IZj1Mg" rel="nofollow noopener">anime lovers.</a> You're welcome.)<br><br><br><br><b>2)</b> <br><a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=B1jaY136B_k&amp;index=3&amp;list=PLEnRczHRfqsLJ6ueKxZYKzmd91ezzK76i" rel="nofollow noopener">The existential crisis.</a> You know when your friends are all feeling great and accomplished and sure of themselves, and then you're just sitting there wondering <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=j0HkSWVsYOw&amp;index=1&amp;list=PLEnRczHRfqsLJ6ueKxZYKzmd91ezzK76i" rel="nofollow noopener">what the hell are you doing with your life?</a> Yep. I know the feeling. But the thing is, you're not alone in this. And maybe life does not have a point and this whole thing is meaningless and ephemeral, but you still have to make the most of it. You still have to do your best to get as close as possible to that tiny confusing thing people call <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=LDG342_AJVE&amp;list=PLEnRczHRfqsLJ6ueKxZYKzmd91ezzK76i&amp;index=2" rel="nofollow noopener">happiness</a>, because this is the only chance we have. And all the time we've wasted on things we didn't really care about, or didn't really want to do? Well, it will never come back. So I hope now you're emotionally scarred enough to listen to my advice. <br><br><br><br><b>3)</b> <br>Here. Have some chocolate. Oh, and a cookie, too. And, maybe a boxed set of all the seasons of Game of Thrones? A first edition of your favorite book? Have some bonus Phil Lester too (also known as: the brightest ray of sunshine.)<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1461085889ra/18822438.gif" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What? That didn't work? Well, fine then, let's try something else. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1461085889ra/18822439.gif" width="280" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now, if you're still wearing that sad pout, my only chance is to go EXTREME and give you the <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=3YIPSjTmPmo&amp;list=PLNq4xYUMjoQAR1p1De-ILhyNFVdqWEc3R" rel="nofollow noopener">one and only cure for sadness.</a> Yes, watch them all. In the right order. You can thank me later. <br><br><br><br><b>4)</b> <br>So, I'm one of those people who literally gets an <i>itch</i> to travel. Airports, train stations and suitcases are all part of my ideal scenario, and I've been to a lot of pretty amazing places, but... sadly, I'm not a millionaire, and I guess neither are you (if you are, though, teach me your secret) and sometimes this makes it pretty difficult for my wanderlust to be sated. (That... was a really weird sentence. Sorry. Moving on...) My ideal trip, you say? Well, first of all I would like to go back to <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=rswFsrMIaR0&amp;index=3&amp;list=PLJ3LjrwGV0VpCXU4d0iI571ur5Cp4aYlv" rel="nofollow noopener">London</a>, because it's one of those places even Londoners can't get enough of. But still, I'm from Europe, and sometimes it's even more exciting when I get to travel the other side of the world - like <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=mBNPUtFBJD0&amp;index=4&amp;list=PLJ3LjrwGV0VpCXU4d0iI571ur5Cp4aYlv" rel="nofollow noopener">New York</a>, for example, how awesome would that be? Or, of course, my ultimate obsession: <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ljZuro77hbI&amp;index=14&amp;list=PLJ3LjrwGV0VpCXU4d0iI571ur5Cp4aYlv" rel="nofollow noopener">Japan</a>. (Yes, more treats for my otaku friends!)<br><br><br><br><b>5)</b> <br>Yes, this is for all the people interested in my actual review. *cough* <i>boooring</i> *cough* I decided to listen to The Amazing Book Is Not on Fire on audiobook, and I strongly recommend you do too, because: a) British accents. I mean, how could anyone resist to that? and, b) Both Dan and Phil have really pleasant voices to listen to, and it's pretty amazing to hear them tell their own story. This is not your typical Youtuber autobiography, but it's just inherently <i>Dan and Phil</i>, with lots of humour, funny bits and pieces and all the little things that we came to love about those two. It was even better than I expected, but what can I say? They always manage to surprise me. So fish your earphones out of your pocket, sit back and <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=kGQsxBLpUT0" rel="nofollow noopener">enjoy!</a><br><br><br><br><br>... aaaand, that's a wrap, you all! If by now I haven't convinced you to jump on the Dan and Phil bandwagon of funny banter, awkwardness and hilarious videos that will make you laugh out loud at the most inappropriate times, then I don't know what would. </span>
  <a data-text-id="4594251830392986610" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1460891886" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1460891886" />
    <a title="Alexxy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/48647071-alexxy"><img alt="Alexxy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577429581p2/48647071.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1460891886?book_show_action=true">Dec 05, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alexxy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alexxy" href="/user/show/48647071-alexxy">Alexxy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/48647071-alexxy?shelf=2015-reads">2015-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1460891886" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11922689807747697560">Before starting the review, let me get one thing straight: Never read memoirs unless you know the person writing it. (And remember, this applies only to celebrity memoirs. It will not work with Anne Frank’s)<br/>I remember I picked up ‘Yes, please!’ because it was a popular read and DNFed it at 30% because I couldn’t care less about Amy Poehler. So, when I got this book, I was afraid. Really really afraid that I’d DNF this one, too. But fortunately, for the sake of my sanity, I actually quite enjoyed</span>
  <span id="freeText11922689807747697560" style="display:none">Before starting the review, let me get one thing straight: Never read memoirs unless you know the person writing it. (And remember, this applies only to celebrity memoirs. It will not work with Anne Frank’s)<br>I remember I picked up ‘Yes, please!’ because it was a popular read and DNFed it at 30% because I couldn’t care less about Amy Poehler. So, when I got this book, I was afraid. Really really afraid that I’d DNF this one, too. But fortunately, for the sake of my sanity, I actually quite enjoyed ‘the amazing book is not on fire’. Here are the reasons why:<br>1.It is written by Dan and Phil. Do I even need to add any more reasons? These guys are AWESOME. They are my babies. The apples of my eyes. My two little cutie pies. I can’t see how I wouldn’t like their book. I mean the only actual difference with their videos is that there’s no voice and picture here. Which wouldn’t be an actual difference if you’re using the audio book.<br>2.I really enjoyed myself. Some parts were so funny, I had to stifle myself down or I would wake my parents with my bursts of laughter. My father would not be happy about it.<br>3.It’s so colorful and pretty, it was a truly nice change from all the black and white pages I always read. Sometimes I would just stare at their pictures, swoon a little….<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450068299ra/17374648.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>OKAY! I think that’s enough. I mean, if you like Dan and Phil and you enjoy their videos, you’ll enjoy this book as well. I’m not saying it was perfect and didn’t have problems. Yes, it did. Sometimes it was boring (I didn’t particularly enjoy one of their trip stories, which was kinda long…). They had gone a little way overboard with the pictures. Some pages were totally unnecessary. The writing was very simple and didn’t contain even the faintest amount of complicated words. Yadda yadda yadda<br><b>Who cares?</b> Some times you just gotta lay back, forget about criticizing things and enjoy yourself a little.<br><br>Here, have some Dan and Phil:<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450068411i/17374671._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="11922689807747697560" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1265414155" />
    <a title="Francesca" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31502192-francesca"><img alt="Francesca" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1588363946p2/31502192.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1265414155?book_show_action=true">Apr 27, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Francesca" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Francesca" href="/user/show/31502192-francesca">Francesca</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/27830083-the-amazing-book-is-not-on-fire">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31502192-francesca?shelf=2015-reading-challenge">2015-reading-challenge</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31502192-francesca?shelf=favourite-nonfictional-people">favourite-nonfictional-people</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1265414155" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13828036965374761054">Actual rating 4.5 stars. If you're completely unfamiliar with Dan and Phil and haven't watched any of their YouTube videos, then I would not recommend reading this book or listening to the audiobook. This book is for fans, whether they're casual fans or they're fans that watch all their videos religiously. The book is hilarious. Their own unique senses of humour shine through and, even though I listened to the audiobook as well as reading it, when I was just reading the book their voices came ac</span>
  <span id="freeText13828036965374761054" style="display:none">Actual rating 4.5 stars. If you're completely unfamiliar with Dan and Phil and haven't watched any of their YouTube videos, then I would not recommend reading this book or listening to the audiobook. This book is for fans, whether they're casual fans or they're fans that watch all their videos religiously. The book is hilarious. Their own unique senses of humour shine through and, even though I listened to the audiobook as well as reading it, when I was just reading the book their voices came across so well just from the writing. This book is one of the few books I've read this year (or listened to) that has genuinely made me laugh out loud and not just breathe slightly heavier through my nose. Seriously, listening to this on the bus was an error as there were so many times that I nearly burst out laughing and had to try and stifle it so that the people on my bus wouldn't think I was crazy. I'm a huge fan of both of them and therefore I will probably always be somewhat biased towards them but they seem like such genuine, lovely people and they bring so much joy to their viewers and their fans. They really care about their fans and it shows. This book has been made with so much effort and care and the hard work they've put into it really paid off. It's an amazing book (it had to be done) and I highly recommend it. I had so much fun reading and listening to it.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13828036965374761054" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1333802602" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1333802602" />
    <a title="Courtney ♡ librarycutie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/33425898-courtney-librarycutie"><img alt="Courtney ♡ librarycutie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597323627p2/33425898.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1333802602?book_show_action=true">Jul 13, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Courtney ♡ librarycutie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Courtney ♡ librarycutie" href="/user/show/33425898-courtney-librarycutie">Courtney ♡ librarycutie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33425898-courtney-librarycutie?shelf=2015">2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33425898-courtney-librarycutie?shelf=audiobooks">audiobooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33425898-courtney-librarycutie?shelf=memoirs">memoirs</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1333802602" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2130058888996043122">I listened to <i>
  <b>The Amazing Book is not on Fire</b>
</i> by Dan Howell and Phil Lester on <b>Audible</b>!<br/><br/>Incase you haven't figured T out by now, I love watching YouTubers, I find it really enjoyable and entertaining, and better than watching tv most times. Dan and Phil are some of my favorites, so I decided to listen to their Audio book, and I wasn't Dissapointed.<br/><br/>I was, however, Dissapointed to see some people give the book 1 or 2 stars, and after reading them they have all been towards the book, not the aud</span>
  <span id="freeText2130058888996043122" style="display:none">I listened to <i>
  <b>The Amazing Book is not on Fire</b>
</i> by Dan Howell and Phil Lester on <b>Audible</b>!<br /><br />Incase you haven't figured T out by now, I love watching YouTubers, I find it really enjoyable and entertaining, and better than watching tv most times. Dan and Phil are some of my favorites, so I decided to listen to their Audio book, and I wasn't Dissapointed.<br /><br />I was, however, Dissapointed to see some people give the book 1 or 2 stars, and after reading them they have all been towards the book, not the audio book. Let me say that I believe the Audiobook is better than the book, <i>and I haven't even read the book</i>, because Dan and Phil is speaking throughout the whole thing, they included sound effects and some music and they even had banters throughout it. I think it's great for anyone who is a fan of Dan and Phil, even though there's been talk my hat there's not a lot of new information about them.<br /><br />I think this Audiobook was Entertaining, humorous, interesting, and definitely enjoyable. I think if you're a fan, you might like the audio book better because of the interactions, but there is the fact that there's photos n the book… maybe buy both?<br /><br />I give this 4 out of 5 stars!</span>
  <a data-text-id="2130058888996043122" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1416248114" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1416248114" />
    <a title="kelsey" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/45903567-kelsey"><img alt="kelsey" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1466982689p2/45903567.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1416248114?book_show_action=true">Oct 14, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="kelsey" class="user" itemprop="url" name="kelsey" href="/user/show/45903567-kelsey">kelsey</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/25487137-the-amazing-book-is-not-on-fire">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/45903567-kelsey?shelf=terrible">terrible</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1416248114" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3930103037624845181">(For people who have trouble downloading this book on their iPhones, try downloading it to your computer. I was only able to read it there; I am not sure if it is ever compatible with the iPhone, but I would imagine that even if you managed to download it there, the text would be unreadable as it was already difficult enough to read full-size on a 15 inch screen!)<br/><br/>I identify as "<b>phan trash</b>" and even I couldn't get through this book. It hurts me to write this review because I really do care about </span>
  <span id="freeText3930103037624845181" style="display:none">(For people who have trouble downloading this book on their iPhones, try downloading it to your computer. I was only able to read it there; I am not sure if it is ever compatible with the iPhone, but I would imagine that even if you managed to download it there, the text would be unreadable as it was already difficult enough to read full-size on a 15 inch screen!)<br /><br />I identify as "<b>phan trash</b>" and even I couldn't get through this book. It hurts me to write this review because I really do care about Dan and Phil as individuals and creators, and I am sure a large reason this book failed to capture my interest was that its age demographic (and admittedly, the grand majority of their fan base) are a great deal <i>younger</i> than I am. Still, the lackluster content of this book was just the beginning of the list of things that disappointed me about it; it was just the tip of the ice berg in my list of complaints, honestly.<br /><br /><b>1. The format</b><br />The format of this book frustrated me to no end! They continually changed from font to different font, all of which were unpleasant on the eyes at best, unreadable at worst. I thought a lot of the art and styling was just downright gaudy, but it also simply seemed to lack cohesiveness. Of course artistic taste varies from individual to individual, but the abrasive change in format from page to page was rather jarring. The page detailing Dan's "dream diaries" stands out in my mind as being extremely unreadable. I guess hardcore fans would be excited to see Dan's handwriting, but I was just frustrated by it as I couldn't read a word of that chicken scratch!<br /><br /><b>2. The "humor"</b><br />I guess it's a matter of taste, but I didn't even catch myself <i>smiling</i> while reading this book. It might be a matter of age demographic, but I was rather shocked as their videos will usual get a smile or a chuckle out of me. I think their visual personalities can make up for the juvenile nature of their jokes/humor. Their jokes may be on the more "random"/"meme" spectrum of humor, but I am able to excuse that in their videos as I find their "banter" and true, more "adult" personalities are able to shine through. All of that is taken away when their ideas are transmitted through the written form, leaving a very simple, disappointing creative product.<br /><br /><b>3. Writing ability</b><br />Sadly, I have to say, writing is not Phil or Dan's forte. Over the years they have developed their ability to make videos and entertain their internet audience, but their startling lack of writing ability (or decision not to showcase it/suppress it here) was very apparent and was a bit surprising. I knew that they would try to keep the material as PG as possible, but I was still expecting writing on a higher level - especially with how much they stressed that they had been working night and day writing this thing, and I was sorely disappointed. The book read like a long rambly tumblr blog or something... it didn't feel like a "book." I guess in my ideal world, their book would have been written in an attractive, readable font, had less unnecessary pictures that we have already seen before, and went into lovely literary detail about some experiences in their lives.<br /><br /><b>4. The content</b><br />This book is written for a very low level of reader, and because of that you would expect it to be easy to get through...not the case whatsoever! This book didn't use any challenging vocabulary and wasn't complex in the least and it was such a chore to read that I just gave up on it after a few pages. This book simply bored me, and I actually care about Dan and Phil's personal lives - I am a <i>fan</i>! I can't imagine how interminable this thing would be to read for someone who knows very little about them!<br /><br />Dan and Phil, as a fan I am saddened to have to write this review, but as I forked over 10 dollars over for a book I couldn't even finish... I am sorry to say that I regret buying this book. If you two ever write a book in the future, I sincerely hope that you will choose to go in a different direction when writing it.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3930103037624845181" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('LFh4U/g9k2o69BPWoqZWjzYy+iHSeZq3R6n0ihoTEEnoeliiGih4/N0fjJBrM4B782zwEch877WxUqK/j1N8NQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('qW2Qk0ysd0a7No92yP2LdG1Sa6vCLNvZwyc5saHqJc9tT7Birrmc0FzdEDABaF2AqAxhm9gprts13G+ENKpJsw==')})
  }

          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: $('box').getStyle('z-index')})});
        } else {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: 6000})});
        }
      });

      newTip['wrapper'].addClassName('prototipAllowOverflow');

        $('bookCover_22921010').observe('prototip:shown', function () {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function (e) {
            if ($('bookCover_22921010').hasClassName('ignored')) {
              e.setStyle({'display': 'none'});
              return;
            }
            e.setStyle({'overflow': 'visible'});
          });
        });
      $('bookCover_22921010').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

//]]>
</script>

</li>
</ul>
